                            <div id='header-search' class='span6 pull-right text-right'>
    <form class='form-inline custom-search-form' action='/search' method='get'>

    <input type='text' class='input-xlarge typeahead' name='q' id='search-input' autocomplete='off' spellcheck='false' placeholder="Search Buildings, Companies, Cities & Countries" style="padding:6px !important; width:330px !important;" />

    </form>

    <script type='text/javascript'>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var algolia = algoliasearch('VQAAT9TYC4', 'eec96cb29df3072743c09f1cbb793281');
        var algoliaCompanies = algolia.initIndex('SC_Companies');
        var algoliaBuildings = algolia.initIndex('SC_Buildings');
        var algoliaComplexes = algolia.initIndex('SC_Complexes');
		
		
		var algoliaCities = algolia.initIndex('v2_cities');
		var algoliaCountries = algolia.initIndex('v2_countries');

        var templateCompany = Hogan.compile('<div class="company"><a href="/company/{{ id }}"><span style="display: block">{{{ _highlightResult.name.value }}}</span></a></div>');
        var templateBuilding = Hogan.compile('<div class="building"><a href="{{ url }}"><span style="display: block">{{{ nameToUse }}}{{{ cityToUse }}}</span></a></div>');
        var templateComplex = Hogan.compile('<div class="complex"><a href="{{ url }}"><span style="display: block">{{{ nameToUse }}}{{{ cityToUse }}}</span></a></div>');

		var templateCity = Hogan.compile('<div class="city"><a href="/city/{{ url_name }}"><span style="display: block">{{ name }}</span></a></div>');
		var templateCountry = Hogan.compile('<div class="country"><a href="/country/{{ url_name }}"><span style="display: block">{{ name }}</span></a></div>');
		
        var typeaheadCtrl = $('#search-input').typeahead({
            minLength: 3,
            hint: false,
            highlight: false
        }, [
        {
            source: algoliaBuildings.ttAdapter({ hitsPerPage: 4, replaceSynonymsInHighlight: false, typoTolerance: 'strict' }),
            displayKey: 'name',
            templates: {
                header: "<div class='category'>Buildings</div>",
                suggestion: function(hit) {
                    var cityToUse = '';
                    var nameToUse = hit._highlightResult.name.value;

                    if (hit.city != '') {
                      cityToUse = ' <small>(' + hit.city + ')</small>';
                    }

                    hit.cityToUse = cityToUse;
                    hit.nameToUse = nameToUse;

                    return templateBuilding.render(hit);
                }
            }
        },
        {
            source: algoliaComplexes.ttAdapter({ hitsPerPage: 3, replaceSynonymsInHighlight: false, typoTolerance: 'strict' }),
            displayKey: 'name',
            templates: {
                header: "<div class='category'>Building Complexes</div>",
                suggestion: function(hit) {
                    var cityToUse = '';
                    var nameToUse = hit._highlightResult.name.value;

                    if (hit.city != '') {
                      cityToUse = ' <small>(' + hit.city + ')</small>';
                    }

                    hit.cityToUse = cityToUse;
                    hit.nameToUse = nameToUse;

                    return templateComplex.render(hit);
                }
            }
        },
        {
            source: algoliaCompanies.ttAdapter({ hitsPerPage: 3, replaceSynonymsInHighlight: false, typoTolerance: 'strict' }),
            displayKey: 'name',
            templates: {
                header: "<div class='category'>Companies</div>",
                suggestion: function(hit) { 
					hit.url = '/company/' + hit.id;
				return templateCompany.render(hit); 
				
				},
            }
        },
		// add CITY + COUNTRY
		{
			source:  algoliaCities.ttAdapter({ hitsPerPage: 3, replaceSynonymsInHighlight: false, typoTolerance: 'strict' }),
            displayKey: 'name',
            templates: {
                header: "<div class='category'>Cities</div>",
                suggestion: function(hit) {
					if(hit.slug){
						hit.url_name = hit.slug;
					} else {
						hit.url_name = hit.name.replace(/ /g, '-').toLowerCase();
					}
					
					return templateCity.render(hit);
				},
            }
		},
		{
			source:  algoliaCountries.ttAdapter({ hitsPerPage: 3, replaceSynonymsInHighlight: false, typoTolerance: 'strict' }),
            displayKey: 'name',
            templates: {
                header: "<div class='category'>Countries</div>",
                suggestion: function(hit) {
					hit.url_name = hit.name.replace(/ /g, '-').toLowerCase();
					return templateCountry.render(hit);
				},
            }
		}
			// this is the end
        ]);

        typeaheadCtrl.on('typeahead:selected', function(evt, data) {
			if (false && typeof data.url === "undefined"){
				alert(JSON.stringify(data));
			} else {
				window.location = 'http://' + window.location.host + data.url;
			}
        });

        // Append view all link
        $('.tt-dropdown-menu').append('<div class="all-results"><a id="view-all-link" href="/search">View all results</a>');

        $('#view-all-link').on('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            window.location = 'http://' + window.location.host + '/search#q=' + $('#search-input').val();
        });

        // Append Algolia credit
        $('.tt-dropdown-menu').append('<div class="powered-by-algoliasearch"><small><em>Powered by</em></small><a href="http://www.algolia.com/?utm_source=skyscrapercenter&amp;utm_medium=link&amp;utm_campaign=skyscrapercenter_search" title="Algolia Realtime Search" target="_blank"><img src="/img/algolia.png" alt="Algolia Realtime Search" width="48" height="15"></a></div>');
    });
    </script>
</div>                    </div>

<script type='text/javascript'>
function getBuildingCity(buildingID) {
	var building = jQuery.grep(buildings, function(element, index) {
		if(element.id === buildingID) {
			return true;
		}

		return false;
	});

	if(!building || building.length === 0) {
		building = jQuery.grep(buildingsComp, function(element, index) {
			if(element.id === buildingID) {
				return true;
			}

			return false;
		});
	}

	if(building !== false && typeof building[0] !== 'undefined') {
		return building[0].city;
	}
}

$(document).ready(function() {
	$('#interactive-form').submit(function(e) {
		var formCanBeSubmitted = true;

		var base_year_difference = Math.abs( parseInt($('#base_max_year').val()) - parseInt($('#base_min_year').val()) );
		var comp_year_difference = Math.abs( parseInt($('#comp_max_year').val()) - parseInt($('#comp_min_year').val()) );

		if($('#base_region').val() == '0' && $('#base_country').val() == '0' && $('#base_city').val() == '0' && parseInt($('#base_height_range').val()) < 3 
		   && base_year_difference > 5) {
			alert('The base criteria selected will have more results than can be properly displayed. Please select a region OR a height of at least 150m OR a year range of at most five years.');

			formCanBeSubmitted = false;
			e.preventDefault();
		}

		if(!$('#skip_comparison').is(":checked") && $('#comp_region').val() == '0' && $('#comp_country').val() == '0' && $('#comp_city').val() == '0' && parseInt($('#comp_height_range').val()) < 3 && comp_year_difference > 5) {
			alert('The comparison criteria selected will have more results than can be properly displayed. Please select a region OR a height of at least 150m OR a year range of at most five years.');

			formCanBeSubmitted = false;
			e.preventDefault();
		}

		if($('[name="output[]"]:checked').length < 1) {
			alert("Please select at least one output to display.");

			formCanBeSubmitted = false;
			e.preventDefault();
		}

		if($('[name="output[]"]:checked').length > 4) {
			alert("To ensure optimal performance, please do not select more than four outputs to display at a time.");

			formCanBeSubmitted = false;
			e.preventDefault();
		}
		
		if(formCanBeSubmitted) {
			$('#loading').removeClass('hidden');
		}
	});

	// Reset button
	$('#btnReset').click(function(e) {
		$('#type').prop('checked', false);
		$('.chkbox-type').prop('checked', false);
		$('#type-building').prop('checked', true);

		$('#status').prop('checked', false);
		$('.chkbox-status').prop('checked', false);
		$('#status-COM').prop('checked', true);
		$('#status-UC').prop('checked', true);
		$('#status-UCT').prop('checked', true);
		$('#status-STO').prop('checked', true);

		$('#material').prop('checked', false);
		$('.chkbox-material').prop('checked', false);

		$('#function').prop('checked', false);
		$('.chkbox-function').prop('checked', false);

		initial_base_country = undefined;
		$('#base_region').val(0).change();
		$('#base_country').val(0).change();
		$('#base_city').val(0).change();

		initial_comp_country = undefined;
		$('#comp_region').val(0).change();
		$('#comp_country').val(0).change();
		$('#comp_city').val(0).change();

		$('#base_height_range').val(4);
		$('#comp_height_range').val(4);

		$('#base_company').val('');
		$('#comp_company').val('');

		$('#base_min_year').val(0);
		$('#base_max_year').val(9999);

		$('#comp_min_year').val(0);
		$('#comp_max_year').val(9999);

		$('#skip_comparison').prop('checked', true);
	});

	// Toggle all checkboxes in the current section
	$('.chkbox-toggle').click(function(e) {
		var checkBoxType = e.target.id;
		var checkBoxes = $('.chkbox-' + checkBoxType);

		checkBoxes.prop('checked', e.target.checked);
	});

			var aTag = $("a[name='results']");
    	$('html,body').animate({scrollTop: aTag.offset().top},'slow');
    
    // Populate dropdowns

    function resetDropdown(dropdownID) {
    	$('#' + dropdownID)
			.find('option')
			.remove()
			.end()
			.append('<option value="0">All</option>')
			.val('All')
			;
    }

    $('#base_region').change(function(e) {
    	var regionID = e.target.value;

    	$.getJSON("/api/region/" + regionID + "/countries", function(result) {
    		resetDropdown('base_country');

			$.each(result, function(index, data) {
		      $("#base_country").append($("<option />").val(data.id).text(data.value));
		    });

			if(typeof initial_base_country != 'undefined') {
				$('#base_country').val(initial_base_country).change();
				initial_base_country = undefined;
			}
		});
    });

    $('#base_country').change(function(e) {
    	var countryID = e.target.value;

    	$.getJSON("/api/country/" + countryID + "/cities", function(result) {
    		resetDropdown('base_city');

			$.each(result, function(index, data) {
		      $("#base_city").append($("<option />").val(data.id).text(data.value));
		    });

			if(typeof initial_base_city != 'undefined') {
				$('#base_city').val(initial_base_city).change();
				initial_base_city = undefined;
			}
		});
    });

    $('#comp_region').change(function(e) {
    	var regionID = e.target.value;

    	$.getJSON("/api/region/" + regionID + "/countries", function(result) {
    		resetDropdown('comp_country');

			$.each(result, function(index, data) {
		      $("#comp_country").append($("<option />").val(data.id).text(data.value));
		    });

			if(typeof initial_comp_country != 'undefined') {
				$('#comp_country').val(initial_comp_country).change();
				initial_comp_country = undefined;
			}
		});
    });

    $('#comp_country').change(function(e) {
    	var countryID = e.target.value;

    	$.getJSON("/api/country/" + countryID + "/cities", function(result) {
    		resetDropdown('comp_city');

			$.each(result, function(index, data) {
		      $("#comp_city").append($("<option />").val(data.id).text(data.value));
		    });

			if(typeof initial_comp_city != 'undefined') {
				$('#comp_city').val(initial_comp_city).change();
				initial_comp_city = undefined;
			}
		});
    });

    // Dropdown defaults

    	    	    		    	    		    	    		    		var initial_base_city = 942;

	    		$('#base_city').val(942).change();
	    		    	    		    	    		    	    		    	
    if(typeof initial_base_region != 'undefined') {
		$('#base_region').val(initial_base_region).change();
	}

	if(typeof initial_comp_region != 'undefined') {
		$('#comp_region').val(initial_comp_region).change();
	}

	$('#copy-criteria').bind('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();

		initial_comp_country = $('#base_country').val();
		initial_comp_city = $('#base_city').val();

		$('#comp_region').val($('#base_region').val()).change();

		var fields = ['height_range', 'company', 'min_year', 'max_year'];

		for(i = 0; i < fields.length; i++) {
			currentField = fields[i];

			$('#comp_' + currentField).val($('#base_' + currentField).val());
		}
	});
});
</script>

	<script type='text/javascript'>
	
	$(document).ready(function() {
		$('#table-baseList').DataTable({
			data: buildings,
			columns: [
				{ data: 'rank' },
				{ data: 'status' },
				{ data: 'name_linked' },
				{ data: 'city' },
				{ data: 'height_architecture_formatted' },
				{ data: 'height_architecture_ft_formatted' },
				{ data: 'floors_above' },
				{ data: 'completed' },
				{ data: 'structural_material' },
				{ data: 'functions' }
			],
			columnDefs: [
				{
					'targets': 1,
					'createdCell': function(td, cellData, rowData, row, col) {
						$(td).addClass('status-' + cellData);
						$(td).html('');
					}
				},
				{
					'targets': 2,
					'createdCell': function(td, cellData, rowData, row, col) {
						$(td).addClass('building-hover');
						$(td).attr('bid', rowData.id);
					}
				},
				{
					'targets': 3,
					'createdCell': function(td, cellData, rowData, row, col) {
													$(td).html("<a href='/city/" + rowData.city_slug + "' target='_blank'>" + cellData + "</a> (<a href='/country/" + rowData.country_slug + "'>" + rowData.country_locode + "</a>)");
											}
				}
			],
			drawCallback: function(s) {
				// Get building IDs present on this page
				var api = this.api();
				var buildingData = api.rows({ page: 'current' }).data();
				var buildingsToGetImages = [];

				$.each(buildingData, function(key, building) {
					if(typeof buildingImages[building.id] === 'undefined') {
						buildingsToGetImages.push(building.id);
					}
				});

				// Populate building images array
				getBuildingImages(buildingsToGetImages);
			},
			pageLength: 50,
			autoWidth: false,
			dom: 'fptp',
					});
	});
	</script>
			
					</div>
	</div>
